*/\n  maxWidth: number\n  /** Maximum height in pixels */\n  maxHeight: number\n}\n\n/**\n * Default window size configuration\n */\nexport const DEFAULT_WINDOW_SIZE: WindowSize = {\n  width: 500,\n  height: 600,\n  minWidth: 380,\n  minHeight: 400,\n  maxWidth: 900,\n  maxHeight: 900,\n}\n\n/**\n * Default window position\n */\nexport const DEFAULT_WINDOW_POSITION: WindowPosition = {\n  x: 20,\n  y: 80,\n  anchor: 'top-right',\n}\n\n/**\n * Window state (open, minimized, pinned)\n */\nexport type WindowState = 'open' | 'minimized' | 'closed'\n\n/**\n * Keyboard shortcuts configuration\n */\nexport interface KeyboardShortcuts {\n  /** Shortcut to toggle GOD MODE window (default: Ctrl+Shift+G) */\n  toggleWindow: string\n  /** Shortcut to minimize window */\n  minimizeWindow?: string\n  /** Shortcut to switch to next tab */\n  nextTab?: string\n  /** Shortcut to switch to previous tab */\n  prevTab?: string\n}\n\n/**\n * Default keyboard shortcuts\n */\nexport const }\n  /** Initial window position */\n  position?: WindowPosition\n  /** Initial window size */\n  size?: Partial<WindowSize>\n  /** Visible tabs (default: all available) */\n  tabs?: GodModeTab[]\n  /** Keyboard shortcuts configuration */\n  shortcuts?: Partial<KeyboardShortcuts>\n  /** Preferred language for UI */\n  preferredLanguage?: QueryLanguage\n  /** Whether to remember window state between sessions */\n  persistState?: boolean\n}\n\n/**\n * Default GOD MODE configuration\n */\nexport const DEFAULT_GOD_MODE_CONFIG: GodModeConfig = {\n  position: DEFAULT_WINDOW_POSITION,\n  size: activeTab: 'query',\n  isPinned: false,\n}\n\n/**\n * LocalStorage key for GOD MODE state\n */\nexport const GOD_MODE_STORAGE_KEY = 'isocubic_god_mode_state'\n\n/**\n * Loads GOD MODE state from localStorage\n */\nexport function loadGodModeState(): GodModeWindowState {\n  try {\n    const stored = localStorage.getItem(GOD_MODE_STORAGE_KEY)\n    if (stored) {\n      const parsed = JSON.parse(stored)\n      return {\n        ...DEFAULT_WINDOW_STATE,\n        ...parsed,\n        position: { ...DEFAULT_WINDOW_POSITION, ...parsed.position },\n        size: { ...DEFAULT_WINDOW_SIZE, ...parsed.size },\n      }\n    }\n  } catch (e) {\n    console.warn('Failed to load GOD MODE state:', e)\n  }\n  return DEFAULT_WINDOW_STATE\n}\n\n/**\n * Saves GOD MODE state to localStorage\n */\nexport function saveGodModeState(state: GodModeWindowState): void {\n  try {\n    localStorage.setItem(GOD_MODE_STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(state))\n  } catch (e) {\n    console.warn('Failed to save GOD MODE state:', e)\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Drag operation state\n */\nexport interface DragState {\n  /** Whether dragging is active */\n  isDragging: boolean\n  /** Starting mouse X position */\n and max values\n */\nexport function clamp(value: number, min: number, max: number): number {\n  return Math.min(Math.max(value, min), max)\n}\n\n/**\n * Ensures window position is within viewport bounds\n */\nexport function constrainPosition(\n  position: WindowPosition,\n  size: WindowSize,\n  viewportWidth: number,\n  viewportHeight: number\n): WindowPosition {\n  const padding = 20\n  return {\n    ...position,\n    x: clamp(position.x, padding, viewportWidth - size.width - padding),\n    y: clamp(position.y, padding, viewportHeight - size.height - padding),\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Ensures window size is within constraints\n */\nexport function constrainSize(size: Partial<WindowSize>): WindowSize {\n  const base = { ...DEFAULT_WINDOW_SIZE, ...size }\n  return {\n    ...base,\n    width: clamp(base.width, base.minWidth, base.maxWidth),\n    height: clamp(base.height, base.minHeight, base.maxHeight),\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Parses keyboard shortcut string into key components\n */\nexport function parseShortcut(shortcut: string): {\n  ctrl: boolean\n  shift: boolean\n  alt: boolean\n  meta: boolean\n  key: string\n} {\n  const parts = shortcut.toLowerCase().split('+')\n  const key = parts[parts.length - 1]\n\n  return {\n    ctrl: parts.includes('ctrl'),\n    shift: parts.includes('shift'),\n    alt: parts.includes('alt'),\n    meta: parts.includes('meta') || parts.includes('cmd'),\n    key,\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Checks if a keyboard event matches a shortcut\n */\nexport function matchesShortcut(event: KeyboardEvent, shortcut: string): boolean {\n  const parsed = parseShortcut(shortcut)\n  return (\n    (parsed.ctrl ? event.ctrlKey || event.metaKey : !event.ctrlKey && !event.metaKey) &&\n    parsed.shift === event.shiftKey &&\n    parsed.alt === event.altKey &&\n    event.key.toLowerCase() === parsed.key\n  )\n}\n\n// =============================================================================\n// TASK 56: Issue Draft Generator Types\n// 'explain', 'question', 'unclear'],\n    },\n  },\n]\n\n/**\n * Generates a unique draft ID\n */\nexport function generateDraftId(): string {\n  return priority: IssuePriority = 'medium'\n): IssueDraft {\n  const now = new Date().toISOString()\n  const template = ISSUE_TEMPLATES.find((t) => t.type === type)\n  \n  return {\n    id: generateDraftId(),\n    title: title || (template ? template.titleTemplate.replace('{summary}', 'New issue') : 'New issue'),\n    body: template ? template.bodyTemplate : '',\n    type,\n    priority,\n    labels: template ? [...template.defaultLabels] : [],\n    screenshots: [],\n    relatedComponents: [],\n    createdAt: now,\n    updatedAt: now,\n    isReady: false,\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Gets priority weight for sorting\n */\nexport function getPriorityWeight(priority: IssuePriority): number {\n  switch (priority) {\n    case 'critical':\n      return 4\n    case 'high':\n      return 3\n    case 'medium':\n      return 2\n    case 'low':\n      return 1\n    default:\n      return 0\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Checks if a draft is valid for publication\n */\nexport function isValidDraft(draft: IssueDraft): boolean {\n 'isocubic_god_mode_issue_draft_settings'\n\n// =============================================================================\n// TASK 55: AI Conversation Agent Types\n// currentView?: string\n  /** Any selected text or code */\n  selectedText?: string\n}\n\n/**\n * A single message in the conversation\n */\nexport interface ConversationMessage {\n  /** Unique message */\nexport function parseShortcut(shortcut: string): {\n  ctrl: boolean\n  shift: boolean\n  alt: boolean\n  meta: boolean\n  key: string\n} {\n  const parts = shortcut.toLowerCase().split('+')\n parts.includes('cmd'),\n    key,\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Checks if a keyboard event matches a shortcut\n */\nexport function matchesShortcut(event: KeyboardEvent, shortcut: string): boolean {\n  const height: number\n  /** Minimum width in pixels */\n  minWidth: number\n  /** Minimum height in pixels */\n  minHeight: number\n  /** Maximum width in pixels */\n  maxWidth: number\n  /** Maximum height in pixels */\n  maxHeight: number\n}\n\n/**\n * Default window size configuration\n */\nexport const DEFAULT_WINDOW_SIZE: WindowSize = {\n  width: 500,\n  height: 600,\n  minWidth: 380,\n  minHeight: 400,\n  maxWidth: 900,\n  maxHeight: 900,\n}\n\n/**\n * Default window position\n */\nexport const DEFAULT_WINDOW_POSITION: WindowPosition = {\n  x: 20,\n  y: 80,\n  anchor: 'top-right',\n}\n\n/**\n * Window state (open, minimized, pinned)\n */\nexport type WindowState = 'open' | 'minimized' | 'closed'\n\n/**\n * Keyboard shortcuts configuration\n */\nexport interface KeyboardShortcuts {\n  /** Shortcut to toggle GOD MODE window (default: Ctrl+Shift+G) */\n  toggleWindow: string\n  /** Shortcut to minimize window */\n  minimizeWindow?: string\n  /** Shortcut to switch to next tab */\n  nextTab?: string\n  /** Shortcut to switch to previous tab */\n  prevTab?: string\n}\n\n/**\n * Default keyboard shortcuts\n */\nexport const DEFAULT_KEYBOARD_SHORTCUTS: KeyboardShortcuts = {\n  toggleWindow: 'Ctrl+Shift+G',\n  minimizeWindow: 'Escape',\n  nextTab: 'Ctrl+Tab',\n  prevTab: 'Ctrl+Shift+Tab',\n}\n\n/**\n * GOD MODE window configuration\n */\nexport interface GodModeConfig {\n  /** GitHub repository owner for issue creation (TASK 57) */\n  github?: {\n    owner: string\n    repo: string\n    defaultLabels?: string[]\n  }\n  /** Initial window position */\n  position?: WindowPosition\n  /** Initial window size */\n  size?: Partial<WindowSize>\n  /** Visible tabs (default: all available) */\n  tabs?: GodModeTab[]\n  /** Keyboard shortcuts configuration */\n  shortcuts?: Partial<KeyboardShortcuts>\n  /** Preferred language for UI */\n  preferredLanguage?: QueryLanguage\n  /** Whether to remember window state between sessions */\n  persistState?: boolean\n}\n\n/**\n * Default GOD MODE configuration\n */\nexport const DEFAULT_GOD_MODE_CONFIG: GodModeConfig = {\n  position: DEFAULT_WINDOW_POSITION,\n  size: DEFAULT_WINDOW_SIZE,\n  tabs: ['query', 'context', 'search'],\n  shortcuts: DEFAULT_KEYBOARD_SHORTCUTS,\n  preferredLanguage: 'ru',\n  persistState: true,\n}\n\n/**\n * GOD MODE window state (for persistence)\n */\nexport interface GodModeWindowState {\n  /** Current window state */\n  state: WindowState\n  /** Current position */\n  position: WindowPosition\n  /** Current size */\n  size: WindowSize\n  /** Currently active tab */\n  activeTab: GodModeTab\n  /** Whether window is pinned (stays on top) */\n  isPinned: boolean\n  /** Last opened timestamp */\n  lastOpened?: string\n}\n\n/**\n * Default window state\n */\nexport const DEFAULT_WINDOW_STATE: GodModeWindowState = {\n  state: 'closed',\n  position: DEFAULT_WINDOW_POSITION,\n  size: DEFAULT_WINDOW_SIZE,\n  activeTab: 'query',\n  isPinned: false,\n}\n\n/**\n * LocalStorage key for GOD MODE state\n */\nexport const GOD_MODE_STORAGE_KEY = 'isocubic_god_mode_state'\n\n/**\n * Loads GOD MODE state from localStorage\n */\nexport function loadGodModeState(): GodModeWindowState {\n  try {\n    const stored = localStorage.getItem(GOD_MODE_STORAGE_KEY)\n    if (stored) {\n      const parsed = JSON.parse(stored)\n      return {\n        ...DEFAULT_WINDOW_STATE,\n        ...parsed,\n        position: { ...DEFAULT_WINDOW_POSITION, ...parsed.position },\n        size: { ...DEFAULT_WINDOW_SIZE, ...parsed.size },\n      }\n    }\n  } catch (e) {\n    console.warn('Failed to load GOD MODE state:', e)\n  }\n  return DEFAULT_WINDOW_STATE\n}\n\n/**\n * Saves GOD MODE state to localStorage\n */\nexport function saveGodModeState(state: GodModeWindowState): void {\n  try {\n    localStorage.setItem(GOD_MODE_STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(state))\n  } catch (e) {\n    console.warn('Failed to save GOD MODE state:', e)\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Drag operation state\n */\nexport interface DragState {\n  /** Whether dragging is active */\n  isDragging: boolean\n  /** Starting mouse X position */\n  startX: number\n  /** Starting mouse Y position */\n  startY: number\n  /** Starting window X position */\n  startWindowX: number\n  /** Starting window Y position */\n  startWindowY: number\n}\n\n/**\n * Resize operation state\n */\nexport interface ResizeState {\n  /** Whether resizing is active */\n  isResizing: boolean\n  /** Resize edge being dragged */\n  edge: 'n' | 's' | 'e' | 'w' | 'ne' | 'nw' | 'se' | 'sw' | null\n  /** Starting mouse X position */\n  startX: number\n  /** Starting mouse Y position */\n  startY: number\n  /** Starting window width */\n  startWidth: number\n  /** Starting window height */\n  startHeight: number\n  /** Starting window X position */\n  startWindowX: number\n  /** Starting window Y position */\n  startWindowY: number\n}\n\n/**\n * GOD MODE context value interface\n */\nexport interface GodModeContextValue {\n  /** Current window state */\n  windowState: GodModeWindowState\n  /** Configuration */\n  config: GodModeConfig\n  /** Open the GOD MODE window */\n  openWindow: () => void\n  /** Close the GOD MODE window */\n  closeWindow: () => void\n  /** Minimize the GOD MODE window */\n  minimizeWindow: () => void\n  /** Toggle window state (open/closed) */\n  toggleWindow: () => void\n  /** Switch to a specific tab */\n  setActiveTab: (tab: GodModeTab) => void\n  /** Update window position */\n  setPosition: (position: WindowPosition) => void\n  /** Update window size */\n  setSize: (size: Partial<WindowSize>) => void\n  /** Toggle pin state */\n  togglePin: () => void\n  /** Reset to default state */\n  resetState: () => void\n  /** Whether window is currently visible */\n  isVisible: boolean\n}\n\n/**\n * Validates a GOD MODE tab ID\n */\nexport function isValidTab(tab: string): tab is GodModeTab {\n  return ['query', 'context', 'search', 'conversation', 'issues'].includes(tab)\n}\n\n/**\n * Gets tab info by ID\n */\nexport function getTabInfo(tabId: GodModeTab): GodModeTabInfo | undefined {\n  return GOD_MODE_TABS.find((tab) => tab.id === tabId)\n}\n\n/**\n * Gets available tabs based on config\n */\nexport function getAvailableTabs(config?: GodModeConfig): GodModeTabInfo[] {\n  const configTabs = config?.tabs || DEFAULT_GOD_MODE_CONFIG.tabs\n  return GOD_MODE_TABS.filter(\n    (tab) => tab.available && (!configTabs || configTabs.includes(tab.id))\n  )\n}\n\n/**\n * Clamps a number between min and max values\n */\nexport function clamp(value: number, min: number, max: number): number {\n  return Math.min(Math.max(value, min), max)\n}\n\n/**\n * Ensures window position is within viewport bounds\n */\nexport function constrainPosition(\n  position: WindowPosition,\n  size: WindowSize,\n  viewportWidth: number,\n  viewportHeight: number\n): WindowPosition {\n  const padding = 20\n  return {\n    ...position,\n    x: clamp(position.x, padding, viewportWidth - size.width - padding),\n    y: clamp(position.y, padding, viewportHeight - size.height - padding),\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Ensures window size is within constraints\n */\nexport function constrainSize(size: Partial<WindowSize>): WindowSize {\n  const base = { ...DEFAULT_WINDOW_SIZE, ...size }\n  return {\n    ...base,\n    width: clamp(base.width, base.minWidth, base.maxWidth),\n    height: clamp(base.height, base.minHeight, base.maxHeight),\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Parses keyboard shortcut string into key components\n */\nexport function parseShortcut(shortcut: string): {\n  ctrl: boolean\n  shift: boolean\n  alt: boolean\n  meta: boolean\n  key: string\n} {\n  const parts = shortcut.toLowerCase().split('+')\n  const key = parts[parts.length - 1]\n\n  return {\n    ctrl: parts.includes('ctrl'),\n    shift: parts.includes('shift'),\n    alt: parts.includes('alt'),\n    meta: parts.includes('meta') || parts.includes('cmd'),\n    key,\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Checks if a keyboard event matches a shortcut\n */\nexport function matchesShortcut(event: KeyboardEvent, shortcut: string): boolean {\n  const parsed = parseShortcut(shortcut)\n  return (\n    (parsed.ctrl ? event.ctrlKey || event.metaKey : !event.ctrlKey && !event.metaKey) &&\n    parsed.shift === event.shiftKey &&\n    parsed.alt === event.altKey &&\n    event.key.toLowerCase() === parsed.key\n  )\n}\n\n// =============================================================================\n// TASK 56: Issue Draft Generator Types\n// =============================================================================\n\n/**\n * Priority levels for GitHub issues\n */\nexport type IssuePriority = 'low' | 'medium' | 'high' | 'explain', 'question', 'unclear'],\n    },\n  },\n]\n\n/**\n * Generates a unique draft ID\n */\nexport function generateDraftId(): string {\n  return `draft_${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 9)}`\n}\n\n/**\n * Creates a new issue draft\n */\nexport function createIssueDraft(\n  title: string,\n  type: IssueType = 'bug',\n  priority: IssuePriority = 'medium'\n): IssueDraft {\n  const now = new Date().toISOString()\n  const template = ISSUE_TEMPLATES.find((t) => t.type === type)\n  \n  return {\n    id: generateDraftId(),\n    title: title || (template ? template.titleTemplate.replace('{summary}', 'New issue') : 'New issue'),\n    body: template ? template.bodyTemplate : '',\n    type,\n    priority,\n    labels: template ? [...template.defaultLabels] : [],\n    screenshots: [],\n    relatedComponents: [],\n    createdAt: now,\n    updatedAt: now,\n    isReady: false,\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Gets priority weight for sorting\n */\nexport function getPriorityWeight(priority: IssuePriority): number {\n  switch (priority) {\n    case 'critical':\n      return 4\n    case 'high':\n      return 3\n    case 'medium':\n      return 2\n    case 'low':\n      return 1\n    default:\n      return 0\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Checks if a draft is valid for publication\n */\nexport function isValidDraft(draft: IssueDraft): boolean {\n  return (\n    draft.title.trim().length > 0 &&\n    draft.body.trim().length > 0 &&\n    draft.type !== undefined &&\n    draft.priority !== undefined\n  )\n}\n\n/**\n * LocalStorage key for issue parts[parts.length - 1]\n\n  return {\n    ctrl: parts.includes('ctrl'),\n    shift: parts.includes('shift'),\n    alt: parts.includes('alt'),\n    meta: parts.includes('meta') || parts.includes('cmd'),\n    key,\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Checks if a keyboard event matches a shortcut\n */\nexport function matchesShortcut(event: KeyboardEvent, shortcut: string): boolean {\n  const boolean\n}\n\n/**\n * Default GOD MODE configuration\n */\nexport const DEFAULT_GOD_MODE_CONFIG: GodModeConfig = {\n  position: DEFAULT_WINDOW_POSITION,\n  size: DEFAULT_WINDOW_SIZE,\n  tabs: ['query', 'context', 'search', 'issues'],\n  shortcuts: DEFAULT_KEYBOARD_SHORTCUTS,\n  preferredLanguage: 'ru',\n  persistState: true,\n}\n\n/**\n * GOD MODE window state (for persistence)\n */\nexport interface GodModeWindowState {\n  /** Current window state */\n  state: WindowState\n  /** Current position */\n  position: WindowPosition\n  /** Current size */\n  size: WindowSize\n  /** Currently active tab */\n  activeTab: GodModeTab\n  /** Whether window is pinned (stays on top) */\n  isPinned: boolean\n  /** Last opened timestamp */\n  lastOpened?: string\n}\n\n/**\n * Default window state\n */\nexport const DEFAULT_WINDOW_STATE: GodModeWindowState = {\n  state: 'closed',\n  position: DEFAULT_WINDOW_POSITION,\n  size: DEFAULT_WINDOW_SIZE,\n  activeTab: 'query',\n  isPinned: false,\n}\n\n/**\n * LocalStorage key for GOD MODE state\n */\nexport const GOD_MODE_STORAGE_KEY = 'isocubic_god_mode_state'\n\n/**\n * Loads GOD MODE state from localStorage\n */\nexport function loadGodModeState(): GodModeWindowState {\n  try {\n    const stored = localStorage.getItem(GOD_MODE_STORAGE_KEY)\n    if (stored) {\n      const parsed = JSON.parse(stored)\n      return {\n        ...DEFAULT_WINDOW_STATE,\n        ...parsed,\n        position: { ...DEFAULT_WINDOW_POSITION, ...parsed.position },\n        size: { ...DEFAULT_WINDOW_SIZE, ...parsed.size },\n      }\n    }\n  } catch (e) {\n    console.warn('Failed to load GOD MODE state:', e)\n  }\n  return DEFAULT_WINDOW_STATE\n}\n\n/**\n * Saves GOD MODE state to localStorage\n */\nexport function saveGodModeState(state: GodModeWindowState): void {\n  try {\n    localStorage.setItem(GOD_MODE_STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(state))\n  } catch (e) {\n    console.warn('Failed to save GOD MODE state:', e)\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Drag operation state\n */\nexport interface DragState {\n  /** Whether dragging is active */\n  isDragging: boolean\n  /** Starting mouse X position */\n  startX: number\n  /** Starting mouse Y position */\n  startY: number\n  /** Starting window X position */\n  startWindowX: number\n  /** Starting window Y position */\n  startWindowY: number\n}\n\n/**\n * Resize operation state\n */\nexport interface ResizeState {\n  /** Whether resizing is active */\n  isResizing: boolean\n  /** Resize edge being dragged */\n  edge: 'n' | 's' | 'e' | 'w' | 'ne' | 'nw' | 'se' | 'sw' | null\n  /** Starting mouse X position */\n  startX: number\n  /** Starting mouse Y position */\n  startY: number\n  /** Starting window width */\n  startWidth: number\n  /** Starting window height */\n  startHeight: number\n  /** Starting window X position */\n  startWindowX: number\n  /** Starting window Y position */\n  startWindowY: number\n}\n\n/**\n * GOD MODE context value interface\n */\nexport interface GodModeContextValue {\n  /** Current window state */\n  windowState: GodModeWindowState\n  /** Configuration */\n  config: GodModeConfig\n  /** Open the GOD MODE window */\n  openWindow: () => void\n  /** Close the GOD MODE window */\n  closeWindow: () => void\n  /** Minimize the GOD MODE window */\n  minimizeWindow: () => void\n  /** Toggle window state (open/closed) */\n  toggleWindow: () => void\n  /** Switch to a specific tab */\n  setActiveTab: (tab: GodModeTab) => void\n  /** Update window position */\n  setPosition: (position: WindowPosition) => void\n  /** Update window size */\n  setSize: (size: Partial<WindowSize>) => void\n  /** Toggle pin state */\n  togglePin: () => void\n  /** Reset to default state */\n  resetState: () => void\n  /** Whether window is currently visible */\n  isVisible: boolean\n}\n\n/**\n * Validates a GOD MODE tab ID\n */\nexport function isValidTab(tab: string): tab is GodModeTab {\n  return ['query', 'context', 'search', 'conversation', 'issues'].includes(tab)\n}\n\n/**\n * Gets tab info by ID\n */\nexport function getTabInfo(tabId: GodModeTab): GodModeTabInfo | undefined {\n  return GOD_MODE_TABS.find((tab) => tab.id === tabId)\n}\n\n/**\n * Gets available tabs based on config\n */\nexport function getAvailableTabs(config?: GodModeConfig): GodModeTabInfo[] {\n  const configTabs = config?.tabs || DEFAULT_GOD_MODE_CONFIG.tabs\n  return GOD_MODE_TABS.filter(\n    (tab) => tab.available && (!configTabs || configTabs.includes(tab.id))\n  )\n}\n\n/**\n * Clamps a number between min and max values\n */\nexport function clamp(value: number, min: number, max: number): number {\n  return Math.min(Math.max(value, min), max)\n}\n\n/**\n * Ensures window position is within viewport bounds\n */\nexport function constrainPosition(\n  position: WindowPosition,\n  size: WindowSize,\n  viewportWidth: number,\n  viewportHeight: number\n): WindowPosition {\n  const padding = 20\n  return {\n    ...position,\n    x: clamp(position.x, padding, viewportWidth - size.width - padding),\n    y: clamp(position.y, padding, viewportHeight - size.height - padding),\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Ensures window size is within constraints\n */\nexport function constrainSize(size: Partial<WindowSize>): WindowSize {\n  const base = { ...DEFAULT_WINDOW_SIZE, ...size }\n  return {\n    ...base,\n    width: clamp(base.width, base.minWidth, base.maxWidth),\n    height: clamp(base.height, base.minHeight, base.maxHeight),\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Parses keyboard shortcut string into key components\n */\nexport function parseShortcut(shortcut: string): {\n  ctrl: boolean\n  shift: boolean\n  alt: boolean\n  meta: boolean\n  key: string\n} {\n  const parts = shortcut.toLowerCase().split('+')\n  const key = parts[parts.length - 1]\n\n  return {\n    ctrl: parts.includes('ctrl'),\n    shift: parts.includes('shift'),\n    alt: parts.includes('alt'),\n    meta: parts.includes('meta') || parts.includes('cmd'),\n    key,\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Checks if a keyboard event matches a shortcut\n */\nexport function matchesShortcut(event: KeyboardEvent, shortcut: string): boolean {\n  const parsed = parseShortcut(shortcut)\n  return (\n    (parsed.ctrl ? event.ctrlKey || event.metaKey : !event.ctrlKey && !event.metaKey) &&\n    parsed.shift === event.shiftKey &&\n    parsed.alt === event.altKey &&\n    event.key.toLowerCase() === parsed.key\n  )\n}\n\n// =============================================================================\n// TASK 56: Issue Draft Generator Types\n// =============================================================================\n\n/**\n * Priority levels for GitHub issues\n */\nexport type IssuePriority = 'low' | 'medium' | 'high' | 'critical'\n\n/**\n * Types of GitHub issues\n */\nexport type IssueType = 'bug' | 'feature' | 'improvement' | 'documentation' | 'question'\n\n/**\n * Screenshot data attached to an issue\n */\nexport priority: IssuePriority = 'medium'\n): IssueDraft {\n  const now = new Date().toISOString()\n  const template = ISSUE_TEMPLATES.find((t) => t.type === type)\n  \n  return {\n    id: generateDraftId(),\n    title: title || (template ? template.titleTemplate.replace('{summary}', 'New issue') : 'New issue'),\n    body: template ? template.bodyTemplate : '',\n    type,\n    priority,\n    labels: template ? */\nexport function getPriorityWeight(priority: IssuePriority): number {\n  switch (priority) {\n    case 'critical':\n      return 4\n    case 'high':\n      return 3\n    case 'medium':\n      return 2\n    case 'low':\n      return 1\n    default:\n      return 0\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Checks if a draft is valid for publication\n */\nexport function isValidDraft(draft: IssueDraft): boolean {\n
